# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 00:28:34.157114

### Base Program

```py
def reverse(x: int) -> int:
    sign = -1 if x < 0 else 1
    x = abs(x)
    res = 0
    while x:
        res = res * 10 + x % 10
        x //= 10
    res *= sign
    return res if -2**31 <= res <= 2**31 - 1 else 0
```

### Input

```json
[7]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def reverse(x: int) -> int:
    sign = -1 if x < 0 else 1
    x = abs(x)
    res = 0
    while x:
        res = res * 10 + x % 10
        x //= 10
    res *= sign
    return res if -2 ** 31 <= res <= 2 ** 31 - 1 else 0
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def reverse(var_0: int) -> int:
    sign = -1 if var_0 < 0 else 1
    var_0 = abs(var_0)
    res = 0
    while var_0:
        res = res * 10 + var_0 % 10
        var_0 //= 10
    res *= sign
    return res if -2 ** 31 <= res <= 2 ** 31 - 1 else 0
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def reverse(x: int) -> int:
    sign = -1 if x < 0 else 1
    x = abs(x)
    res = 0
    while x:
        res = x % 10 + 10 * res
        x //= 10
    res *= sign
    return res if -2 ** 31 <= res <= 2 ** 31 + -1 else 0
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def reverse(var_1: int) -> int:
    sign = -1 if var_1 < 0 else 1
    var_1 = abs(var_1)
    res = 0
    while var_1:
        res = var_1 % 10 + 10 * res
        var_1 //= 10
    res *= sign
    return res if -2 ** 31 <= res <= 2 ** 31 + -1 else 0
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

Message: 
```
Success
```
